    FROM "Posts" AS "p"
    WHERE "p"."IsPublished" AND "p"."IsFavourite" = @__pickFavourite_0
    ORDER BY "p"."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1
) AS "t"
LEFT JOIN "PostImages" AS "p0" ON "t"."FeaturedImageId" = "p0"."Id"
ORDER BY "t"."CreatedAt" DESC
